# Google Search Console 手动提交指南

**生成时间**: 2026-06-17 08:16:59
**总计文章数**: 75

## 第一步：确认 GSC 站点

1. 打开 [Google Search Console](https://search.google.com/search-console)
2. 左上角选择你的 **aitoolbits.blogspot.com** 站点
3. 如果找不到，点击左上角 ▼ 下拉选择，或重新添加

## 第二步：提交 Sitemap

1. 左侧菜单点击 **编制索引** → **Sitemaps**
2. 在右侧 "添加新 Sitemap" 输入: `sitemap.xml`
3. 点击 **提交**

## 第三步：URL 检查工具逐个提交

对于每篇文章:
1. 复制下方 URL 列表
2. 在 GSC 顶部搜索框粘贴 URL
3. 点击 **测试live网址数据**
4. 如果显示可用，点击 **请求编入索引**

<h3 class='post-title entry-title'>
<a href='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/ai-legal-tools-how-ai-is-changing-legal.html'>AI Legal Tools: How AI Is Changing the Legal Industry</a>
</h3>
</div>
<div class='post-header-container container'>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'>
<span class='byline post-timestamp'>
<meta content='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/ai-legal-tools-how-ai-is-changing-legal.html'/>

<div class='snippet-item r-snippetized'>
The End of Billable Hour Tyranny? How AI Legal Tools Are Reshaping Law         Photo by Unsplash  via Pexels    If you&#8217;re a lawyer, paralegal, or even a solo practitioner, you know the crushing weight of document review. You&#8217;ve lived the late nights sifting through thousands of emails for a single piece of evidence. The legal profession has historically been slow to adopt new tech, but the tide has turned. The rise of AI legal tools  is not a future prediction&#8212;it is a current reality. These platforms are automating the grunt work, slashing research time, and making high-quality legal services accessible to more people than ever before.   In this guide, I&#8217;m cutting through the hype. I&#8217;ve tested dozens of these platforms, looked at their pricing models, and evaluated their impact on actual workflows. Whether you&#8217;re looking to automate contract analysis, draft briefs faster, or manage discovery with fewer associates, this list covers the best legal AI  solutions available right now. We ar...

So I Checked Out ECC...         Photo by Unsplash  via Pexels    Okay, I&#39;ll be real with you. When I first saw a GitHub repo with 216,348 stars  pop up, I was suspicious. That&#39;s not normal. That&#39;s &quot;every developer on Earth has starred this&quot; territory. So I clicked on affaan-m/ECC  expecting either some blockchain scam or a meme project. Instead, I found something that actually made me go &quot;huh, that&#39;s actually useful.&quot;   The name &quot;ECC&quot; sounds like some obscure crypto thing, but it&#39;s not. It&#39;s short for what they call &quot;agent harness performance optimization.&quot; Basically, it&#39;s a tool that sits on top of your AI coding assistants&#8212;Claude Code, Cursor, Codex, Opencode&#8212;and tries to make them way more effective. Think of it as giving your AI agent a brain upgrade.   I&#39;ve been burned by too many &quot;AI agent frameworks&quot; that promise the moon and deliver a half-baked script that doesn&#39;t work with anything. But this...

Why You Need an AI Video Translator Now         Photo by Unsplash  via Pexels   You&#8217;ve got a great video&#8212;maybe a product demo, a tutorial, or a vlog&#8212;but it&#8217;s only in one language. That&#8217;s a massive missed opportunity. Studies show that videos with multilingual subtitles or dubbing can increase viewership by up to 300% in non-English markets. The traditional route? Hire voice actors, translators, and audio engineers. That takes weeks and costs thousands.  That&#8217;s where an AI video translator  changes the game. These tools use advanced speech recognition, neural machine translation, and voice cloning to dub your video into any language in minutes. The best video dubbing AI  tools can even match the original speaker&#8217;s tone, emotion, and timing. Whether you&#8217;re a YouTuber, a course creator, or a marketer, creating a multilingual video  strategy is now easier and cheaper than ever. Let&#8217;s break down the top tools, what they cost, and which one fits your workflow.   How to Choose the Right AI Vi...

<h3 class='post-title entry-title'>
<a href='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/ai-data-visualization-tools-turn-data.html'>AI Data Visualization Tools: Turn Data into Beautiful Charts</a>
</h3>
</div>
<div class='post-header-container container'>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'>
<span class='byline post-timestamp'>
<meta content='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/ai-data-visualization-tools-turn-data.html'/>
<a class='timestamp-link' href='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/ai-data-visualization-tools-turn-data.html' rel='bookmark' title='permanent link'>

<div class='snippet-item r-snippetized'>
Why Your Spreadsheets Are Holding You Back (And How AI Can Fix That)         Photo by Unsplash  via Pexels    Let&#8217;s be honest: staring at a wall of numbers in a spreadsheet is rarely inspiring. You know there&#8217;s a story in that data&#8212;a trend, an insight, a billion-dollar opportunity&#8212;but translating rows and columns into a compelling narrative takes time, design skill, and patience. That&#8217;s where AI data visualization  comes in. These tools are not just about making things pretty; they are about democratizing data analysis. A good chart generator AI  can take raw CSV files and produce publication-ready charts in seconds, allowing you to focus on the &quot;why&quot; instead of the &quot;how.&quot;   The market for data viz AI  has exploded in the last 18 months. We&#8217;ve moved past basic bar charts into a world where AI can suggest the best chart type for your dataset, automatically color-code for accessibility, and even write the narrative around the visualization. But with dozens of tools cl...

<h3 class='post-title entry-title'>
<a href='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/ecc-ai-repo-gaining-215688-stars-this.html'>ECC: The AI Repo Gaining 215,688+ Stars This Week</a>
</h3>
</div>
<div class='post-header-container container'>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'>
<span class='byline post-timestamp'>
<meta content='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/ecc-ai-repo-gaining-215688-stars-this.html'/>
<a class='timestamp-link' href='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/ecc-ai-repo-gaining-215688-stars-this.html' rel='bookmark' title='permanent link'>

<div class='snippet-item r-snippetized'>
So I Checked Out ECC...         Photo by Unsplash  via Pexels   I&#39;ll be honest - when I first saw affaan-m/ECC  sitting at 215,688 stars on GitHub , I did a double-take. That&#39;s not just &quot;popular.&quot; That&#39;s viral territory. The kind of numbers you usually see on projects that have been around for years or are backed by a big company. So naturally, I had to see what the hype was about.  I clicked through, scanned the README, and the first thing that jumped out was the tagline: &quot;The agent harness performance optimization system.&quot; Sounded fancy. But also sounded like something that could be either genius or over-engineered fluff. I&#39;ve been burned before by projects with huge star counts that turned out to be mostly marketing.  So I cloned it. Installed it. Poked around. And now I&#39;m back to tell you what I actually think - not what the README wants you to think.   What It Actually Does  Okay, so here&#39;s the pitch in plain English: ECC is a system tha...

<h3 class='post-title'><a href='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/canva-ai-vs-adobe-firefly-which-design.html'>Canva AI vs Adobe Firefly: Which Design Tool Should You Use?</a></h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'>
<span class='byline post-timestamp'>
<meta content='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/canva-ai-vs-adobe-firefly-which-design.html'/>
<a class='timestamp-link' href='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/canva-ai-vs-adobe-firefly-which-design.html' rel='bookmark' title='permanent link'>
<time class='published' datetime='2026-06-17T02:15:00+08:00' title='2026-06-17T02:15:00+08:00'>

<div class='hero-post-snippet snippet-container r-snippet-container'>
<div class='snippet-item r-snippetized'>
The Great AI Design Showdown: Canva AI vs Adobe Firefly         Photo by Unsplash  via Pexels    You&#8217;ve probably been there. You need a stunning visual for a social post, a blog header, or a client presentation, but you&#8217;re staring at a blank canvas. The pressure is on to create something that looks professional, not amateur. The rise of AI design  tools promises to solve this, but which one actually delivers? The battle between Canva AI  and Adobe Firefly  is the defining rivalry in the AI design space right now. Choosing the wrong one could mean wasted time, money, or worse&#8212;mediocre output.   In this Canva AI vs Adobe Firefly  comparison, I&#8217;m going to break down exactly where each platform shines and where it falls flat. We&#8217;ll look at pricing, core features, real-world use cases, and the hidden limitations that the marketing gloss often hides. By the end, you&#8217;ll know which AI design comparison  winner fits your workflow, budget, and creative ambition. Let&#8217;s cut through the noise.     ...
</div>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title'>

The End of Billable Hour Tyranny? How AI Legal Tools Are Reshaping Law         Photo by Unsplash  via Pexels    If you&#8217;re a lawyer, paralegal, or even a solo practitioner, you know the crushing weight of document review. You&#8217;ve lived the late nights sifting through thousands of emails for a single piece of evidence. The legal profession has historically been slow to adopt new tech, but the tide has turned. The rise of AI legal tools  is not a future prediction&#8212;it is a current reality. These platforms are automating the grunt work, slashing research time, and making high-quality legal services accessible to more people than ever before.   In this guide, I&#8217;m cutting through the hype. I&#8217;ve tested dozens of these platforms, looked at their pricing models, and evaluated their impact on actual workflows. Whether you&#8217;re looking to automate contract analysis, draft briefs faster, or manage discovery with fewer associates, this list covers the best legal AI  solutions available right now. We ar...

So I Checked Out ECC...         Photo by Unsplash  via Pexels    Okay, I&#39;ll be real with you. When I first saw a GitHub repo with 216,348 stars  pop up, I was suspicious. That&#39;s not normal. That&#39;s &quot;every developer on Earth has starred this&quot; territory. So I clicked on affaan-m/ECC  expecting either some blockchain scam or a meme project. Instead, I found something that actually made me go &quot;huh, that&#39;s actually useful.&quot;   The name &quot;ECC&quot; sounds like some obscure crypto thing, but it&#39;s not. It&#39;s short for what they call &quot;agent harness performance optimization.&quot; Basically, it&#39;s a tool that sits on top of your AI coding assistants&#8212;Claude Code, Cursor, Codex, Opencode&#8212;and tries to make them way more effective. Think of it as giving your AI agent a brain upgrade.   I&#39;ve been burned by too many &quot;AI agent frameworks&quot; that promise the moon and deliver a half-baked script that doesn&#39;t work with anything. But this...

Why You Need an AI Video Translator Now         Photo by Unsplash  via Pexels   You&#8217;ve got a great video&#8212;maybe a product demo, a tutorial, or a vlog&#8212;but it&#8217;s only in one language. That&#8217;s a massive missed opportunity. Studies show that videos with multilingual subtitles or dubbing can increase viewership by up to 300% in non-English markets. The traditional route? Hire voice actors, translators, and audio engineers. That takes weeks and costs thousands.  That&#8217;s where an AI video translator  changes the game. These tools use advanced speech recognition, neural machine translation, and voice cloning to dub your video into any language in minutes. The best video dubbing AI  tools can even match the original speaker&#8217;s tone, emotion, and timing. Whether you&#8217;re a YouTuber, a course creator, or a marketer, creating a multilingual video  strategy is now easier and cheaper than ever. <h3 class='post-title entry-title'>
<a href='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/ai-data-visualization-tools-turn-data.html'>AI Data Visualization Tools: Turn Data into Beautiful Charts</a>
</h3>
</div>
<div class='post-header-container container'>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'>

Why Your Spreadsheets Are Holding You Back (And How AI Can Fix That)         Photo by Unsplash  via Pexels    Let&#8217;s be honest: staring at a wall of numbers in a spreadsheet is rarely inspiring. You know there&#8217;s a story in that data&#8212;a trend, an insight, a billion-dollar opportunity&#8212;but translating rows and columns into a compelling narrative takes time, design skill, and patience. That&#8217;s where AI data visualization  comes in. These tools are not just about making things pretty; they are about democratizing data analysis. A good chart generator AI  can take raw CSV files and produce publication-ready charts in seconds, allowing you to focus on the &quot;why&quot; instead of the &quot;how.&quot;   The market for data viz AI  has exploded in the last 18 months. We&#8217;ve moved past basic bar charts into a world where AI can suggest the best chart type for your dataset, automatically color-code for accessibility, and even write the narrative around the visualization. <div class='post-title-container'>
<a name='4421131929392346669'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title'>
<a href='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/ecc-ai-repo-gaining-215688-stars-this.html'>ECC: The AI Repo Gaining 215,688+ Stars This Week</a>
</h3>
</div>
<div class='post-header-container container'>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'>
<span class='byline post-timestamp'>
<meta content='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/ecc-ai-repo-gaining-215688-stars-this.html'/>
<a class='timestamp-link' href='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/ecc-ai-repo-gaining-215688-stars-this.html' rel='bookmark' title='permanent link'>
<time class='published' datetime='2026-06-15T15:30:00+08:00' title='2026-06-15T15:30:00+08:00'>
June 15, 2026
</time>
</a>
</span>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class='container post-body entry-content' id='post-snippet-4421131929392346669'>
<div class='post-snippet snippet-container r-snippet-container'>
<div class='snippet-item r-snippetized'>
So I Checked Out ECC...         Photo by Unsplash  via Pexels   I&#39;ll be honest - when I first saw affaan-m/ECC  sitting at 215,688 stars on GitHub , I did a double-take. That&#39;s not just &quot;popular.&quot; That&#39;s viral territory. The kind of numbers you usually see on projects that have been around for years or are backed by a big company. So naturally, I had to see what the hype was about.  I clicked through, scanned the README, and the first thing that jumped out was the tagline: &quot;The agent harness performance optimization system.&quot; Sounded fancy. But also sounded like something that could be either genius or over-engineered fluff. I&#39;ve been burned before by projects with huge star counts that turned out to be mostly marketing.  So I cloned it. Installed it. Poked around. And now I&#39;m back to tell you what I actually think - not what the README wants you to think.   What It Actually Does  Okay, so here&#39;s the pitch in plain English: ECC is a system tha...
</div>
<a class='snippet-fade r-snippet-fade hidden' href='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/ecc-ai-repo-gaining-215688-stars-this.html'></a>

<a name='72157534102474596'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title'>
<a href='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/canva-ai-vs-adobe-firefly-which-design.html'>Canva AI vs Adobe Firefly: Which Design Tool Should You Use?</a>
</h3>
</div>
<div class='post-header-container container'>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'>
<span class='byline post-timestamp'>
<meta content='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/canva-ai-vs-adobe-firefly-which-design.html'/>
<a class='timestamp-link' href='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/canva-ai-vs-adobe-firefly-which-design.html' rel='bookmark' title='permanent link'>
<time class='published' datetime='2026-06-17T02:15:00+08:00' title='2026-06-17T02:15:00+08:00'>
June 17, 2026
</time>
</a>
</span>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class='container post-body entry-content' id='post-snippet-72157534102474596'>
<div class='post-snippet snippet-container r-snippet-container'>
<div class='snippet-item r-snippetized'>
The Great AI Design Showdown: Canva AI vs Adobe Firefly         Photo by Unsplash  via Pexels    You&#8217;ve probably been there. You need a stunning visual for a social post, a blog header, or a client presentation, but you&#8217;re staring at a blank canvas. The pressure is on to create something that looks professional, not amateur. The rise of AI design  tools promises to solve this, but which one actually delivers? The battle between Canva AI  and Adobe Firefly  is the defining rivalry in the AI design space right now. Choosing the wrong one could mean wasted time, money, or worse&#8212;mediocre output.   In this Canva AI vs Adobe Firefly  comparison, I&#8217;m going to break down exactly where each platform shines and where it falls flat. We&#8217;ll look at pricing, core features, real-world use cases, and the hidden limitations that the marketing gloss often hides. By the end, you&#8217;ll know which AI design comparison  winner fits your workflow, budget, and creative ambition. Let&#8217;s cut through the noise.     ...
</div>
<a class='snippet-fade r-snippet-fade hidden' href='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/canva-ai-vs-adobe-firefly-which-design.html'></a>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title'>
<a href='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/ai-legal-tools-how-ai-is-changing-legal.html'>AI Legal Tools: How AI Is Changing the Legal Industry</a>
</h3>
</div>
<div class='post-header-container container'>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'>
<span class='byline post-timestamp'>
<meta content='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/ai-legal-tools-how-ai-is-changing-legal.html'/>
<a class='timestamp-link' href='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/ai-legal-tools-how-ai-is-changing-legal.html' rel='bookmark' title='permanent link'>

<div class='snippet-item r-snippetized'>
The End of Billable Hour Tyranny? How AI Legal Tools Are Reshaping Law         Photo by Unsplash  via Pexels    If you&#8217;re a lawyer, paralegal, or even a solo practitioner, you know the crushing weight of document review. You&#8217;ve lived the late nights sifting through thousands of emails for a single piece of evidence. The legal profession has historically been slow to adopt new tech, but the tide has turned. The rise of AI legal tools  is not a future prediction&#8212;it is a current reality. These platforms are automating the grunt work, slashing research time, and making high-quality legal services accessible to more people than ever before.   In this guide, I&#8217;m cutting through the hype. I&#8217;ve tested dozens of these platforms, looked at their pricing models, and evaluated their impact on actual workflows. Whether you&#8217;re looking to automate contract analysis, draft briefs faster, or manage discovery with fewer associates, this list covers the best legal AI  solutions available right now. We ar...

<h3 class='post-title entry-title'>
<a href='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/ecc-ai-repo-gaining-216348-stars-this.html'>ECC: The AI Repo Gaining 216,348+ Stars This Week</a>
</h3>
</div>
<div class='post-header-container container'>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'>
<span class='byline post-timestamp'>
<meta content='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/ecc-ai-repo-gaining-216348-stars-this.html'/>
<a class='timestamp-link' href='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/ecc-ai-repo-gaining-216348-stars-this.html' rel='bookmark' title='permanent link'>
<time class='published' datetime='2026-06-16T15:47:00+08:00' title='2026-06-16T15:47:00+08:00'>
June 16, 2026
</time>
</a>
</span>
</div>
</div>

<div class='container post-body entry-content' id='post-snippet-2474487758758628465'>
<div class='post-snippet snippet-container r-snippet-container'>
<div class='snippet-item r-snippetized'>
So I Checked Out ECC...         Photo by Unsplash  via Pexels    Okay, I&#39;ll be real with you. When I first saw a GitHub repo with 216,348 stars  pop up, I was suspicious. That&#39;s not normal. That&#39;s &quot;every developer on Earth has starred this&quot; territory. So I clicked on affaan-m/ECC  expecting either some blockchain scam or a meme project. Instead, I found something that actually made me go &quot;huh, that&#39;s actually useful.&quot;   The name &quot;ECC&quot; sounds like some obscure crypto thing, but it&#39;s not. It&#39;s short for what they call &quot;agent harness performance optimization.&quot; Basically, it&#39;s a tool that sits on top of your AI coding assistants&#8212;Claude Code, Cursor, Codex, Opencode&#8212;and tries to make them way more effective. Think of it as giving your AI agent a brain upgrade.   I&#39;ve been burned by too many &quot;AI agent frameworks&quot; that promise the moon and deliver a half-baked script that doesn&#39;t work with anything. But this...

<h3 class='post-title entry-title'>

The landscape has shifted dramatically. I&#8217;ve spent the last six months testing every major tool on the market, from the established giants to the scrappy newcomers. If you are a developer, a startup founder, or even a hobbyist learning Python, the choice of your AI programmer is arguably the most important tech decision you will make this year.   In this comprehensive comparison, I&#8217;ll break down the top contenders: Cursor AI , GitHub Copilot , Replit , Bolt.new , and Lovable . I&#8217;ll share specific pricing, real-world performance data, and the gritty details that most reviews gloss over. Why You Need an AI Video Translator Now         Photo by Unsplash  via Pexels   You&#8217;ve got a great video&#8212;maybe a product demo, a tutorial, or a vlog&#8212;but it&#8217;s only in one language. That&#8217;s a massive missed opportunity. Studies show that videos with multilingual subtitles or dubbing can increase viewership by up to 300% in non-English markets. The traditional route? Hire voice actors, translators, and audio engineers. That takes weeks and costs thousands.  That&#8217;s where an AI video translator  changes the game. These tools use advanced speech recognition, neural machine translation, and voice cloning to dub your video into any language in minutes. The best video dubbing AI  tools can even match the original speaker&#8217;s tone, emotion, and timing. Whether you&#8217;re a YouTuber, a course creator, or a marketer, creating a multilingual video  strategy is now easier and cheaper than ever. Let&#8217;s break down the top tools, what they cost, and which one fits your workflow.   How to Choose the Right AI Vi...

<h3 class='post-title entry-title'>
<a href='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/ai-data-visualization-tools-turn-data.html'>AI Data Visualization Tools: Turn Data into Beautiful Charts</a>
</h3>
</div>
<div class='post-header-container container'>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'>
<span class='byline post-timestamp'>
<meta content='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/ai-data-visualization-tools-turn-data.html'/>
<a class='timestamp-link' href='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/ai-data-visualization-tools-turn-data.html' rel='bookmark' title='permanent link'>
<time class='published' datetime='2026-06-15T21:12:00+08:00' title='2026-06-15T21:12:00+08:00'>
June 15, 2026
</time>

<div class='post-snippet snippet-container r-snippet-container'>
<div class='snippet-item r-snippetized'>
Why Your Spreadsheets Are Holding You Back (And How AI Can Fix That)         Photo by Unsplash  via Pexels    Let&#8217;s be honest: staring at a wall of numbers in a spreadsheet is rarely inspiring. You know there&#8217;s a story in that data&#8212;a trend, an insight, a billion-dollar opportunity&#8212;but translating rows and columns into a compelling narrative takes time, design skill, and patience. That&#8217;s where AI data visualization  comes in. These tools are not just about making things pretty; they are about democratizing data analysis. A good chart generator AI  can take raw CSV files and produce publication-ready charts in seconds, allowing you to focus on the &quot;why&quot; instead of the &quot;how.&quot;   The market for data viz AI  has exploded in the last 18 months. We&#8217;ve moved past basic bar charts into a world where AI can suggest the best chart type for your dataset, automatically color-code for accessibility, and even write the narrative around the visualization. But with dozens of tools cl...

<h3 class='post-title entry-title'>
<a href='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/ecc-ai-repo-gaining-215688-stars-this.html'>ECC: The AI Repo Gaining 215,688+ Stars This Week</a>
</h3>
</div>
<div class='post-header-container container'>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'>
<span class='byline post-timestamp'>
<meta content='https://aitoolbits.blogspot.com/2026/06/ecc-ai-repo-gaining-215688-stars-this.html'/>

<div class='snippet-item r-snippetized'>
So I Checked Out ECC...         Photo by Unsplash  via Pexels   I&#39;ll be honest - when I first saw affaan-m/ECC  sitting at 215,688 stars on GitHub , I did a double-take. That&#39;s not just &quot;popular.&quot; That&#39;s viral territory. The kind of numbers you usually see on projects that have been around for years or are backed by a big company. So naturally, I had to see what the hype was about.  I clicked through, scanned the README, and the first thing that jumped out was the tagline: &quot;The agent harness performance optimization system.&quot; Sounded fancy. But also sounded like something that could be either genius or over-engineered fluff. I&#39;ve been burned before by projects with huge star counts that turned out to be mostly marketing.  So I cloned it. Installed it. Poked around. And now I&#39;m back to tell you what I actually think - not what the README wants you to think.   What It Actually Does  Okay, so here&#39;s the pitch in plain English: ECC is a system tha...
